This is an abstract admission plugin that provides common infrastructure for both mutating and validating webhooks. The key methods are:\\n\\n- `Dispatch()`: Routes webhook calls to the appropriate dispatcher based on admission attributes\\n- `ShouldCallHook()`: Determines whether a specific webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\nThe `generic/interfaces.go` file defines critical abstractions:\\n- `Dispatcher`: An interface for dispatching webhook calls to a list of webhooks\\n- `Source`: Provides dynamic list of webhooks from configurations\\n- `WebhookInvocation`: Describes how to call a webhook, including resource and subresource information\\n- `VersionedAttributeAccessor`: Manages versioned attributes for different webhook kinds\\n\\n## WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer\\n\\nIn `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`, the `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified abstraction for both mutating and validating webhooks. This abstraction allows code to work with either type without type-specific logic. Key implementations include:\\n\\n- `mutatingWebhookAccessor`: Wraps `v1.MutatingWebhook` objects\\n- `validatingWebhookAccessor`: Wraps `v1.ValidatingWebhook` objects\\n\\nFactory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor` create appropriately typed accessors with cached label selectors and compiled match conditions.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Pipeline\\n\\nThe mutating webhook pipeline starts in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`, where the `Plugin` struct embeds the generic `Webhook`. The `Admit()` method calls the generic `Dispatch()`, which delegates to `mutatingDispatcher`.\\n\\nThe `mutatingDispatcher` in `dispatcher.go` implements reinvocation logic for mutating webhooks:\\n- Uses `webhookReinvokeContext` to track which webhooks have been invoked\\n- Implements the `ReinvocationPolicy` mechanism to support re-invocation when mutations occur\\n- Processes webhooks serially (one after another) to ensure predictable mutation ordering\\n- Applies JSON patches from webhook responses to the object\\n- Tracks patch audit annotations for each webhook invocation\\n- Supports failure policy (Ignore or Fail)\\n\\nKey algorithm: The dispatcher iterates through hooks, calls `ShouldCallHook()` for each, and if eligible, calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` which constructs the AdmissionReview, sends it to the webhook endpoint, verifies the response, and applies any patches to the request object.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Pipeline\\n\\nThe validating webhook pipeline starts in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`, similar to mutating. However, the `validatingDispatcher` in `dispatcher.go` uses **parallel dispatch** via goroutines:\\n\\n- Creates a list of relevant hooks by pre-filtering with `ShouldCallHook()`\\n- Pre-caches all versioned attributes to avoid repeated conversions\\n- Spawns goroutines in a `sync.WaitGroup` for each webhook\\n- Each goroutine independently calls its webhook via `callHook()`\\n- Collects errors in a channel for centralized error handling\\n- Includes panic recovery and crash handling per goroutine\\n- Supports failure policy (Ignore or Fail) with independent evaluation per goroutine\\n\\nThis parallel design improves latency since validating webhooks don't modify the object.\\n\\n## Configuration Management\\n\\nThe configuration managers in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/` serve as the `Source` for webhooks:\\n\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager`: Reads `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` objects from a Kubernetes informer, creates `mutatingWebhookAccessor` instances, maintains a cache, and provides sorted lists of webhooks\\n- `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager`: Similarly manages `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` objects\\n\\nBoth managers implement:\\n- Lazy evaluation of webhook configurations\\n- Caching of created webhook accessors (expensive due to CEL expression compilation)\\n- Event handlers for Add/Update/Delete of configurations\\n- Deterministic ordering of webhooks across configurations\\n\\n## API Type Definitions\\n\\nIn `admissionregistration/v1/types.go` and `admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go`, the Kubernetes API defines:\\n\\n- `MutatingWebhookConfiguration`: A cluster-scoped resource containing multiple `MutatingWebhook` objects. Each webhook specifies rules, failure policy, client configuration, reinvocation policy, side effects, and match conditions.\\n- `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration`: A cluster-scoped resource containing multiple `ValidatingWebhook` objects with similar fields but no reinvocation policy.\\n- `MutatingWebhook` and `ValidatingWebhook`: Individual webhook specifications with support for namespace/object selectors, rule matching, and CEL-based match conditions.\\n\\n## Processing Flow Summary\\n\\n**Mutating Webhooks**:\\n1. Plugin.Admit() → Webhook.Dispatch() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch()\\n2. Serial processing of webhooks (deterministic ordering)\\n3. Each webhook may modify the object (patch)\\n4. Reinvocation support when objects change\\n5. Result: Modified object passed to next plugin\\n\\n**Validating Webhooks**:\\n1. Plugin.Validate() → Webhook.Dispatch() → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch()\\n2. Parallel processing of webhooks (spawn goroutines)\\n3. Each webhook validates without modification\\n4. First error returned (early failure)\\n5. Result: Accept/reject decision\\n\\nBoth pipelines share the same generic webhook matching logic (ShouldCallHook) and WebhookAccessor abstraction, ensuring consistent behavior across mutating and validating webhooks while allowing pipeline-specific optimizations.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2266,"cache_read_input_tokens":88543,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2266},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6aafa745-8dbe-40fe-9bf2-f010116165f1","uuid":"af0378d5-4e66-4de4-97bd-578896c3ddec"}
